			- Пусть N – цена 1 человеческой жизни для разумного человечества (разумное человечество — человечество на такой стадии развития, при которой выполняется данная теорема), тогда N → ∞ по определению жизни ⇒  цена смерти (смерть — такой процесс в организме, при котором v→ 0, где v — скорость жизни, где жизнь — процесс восприятия, специфической обработки и хранения информации (организм — есть некая субстанция, в которой происходят процессы, характерные для жизни)) → -∞ (цена для разумного человечества - есть убыток, который она понесет при потере данного объекта, либо явления). Пусть Q — максимальные затраты всех форм, необходимые для реализации плана «вечность» (план «вечность» - есть совокупность действий, мер, направленных на  v→const != 0 у данного организма на t →∞ (t - время), причем заведомо Q << ∞ (Q выражено в тех же единицах, что и N) ⇒ Q  << N всегда. Таким образом выполнение плана «вечность» - есть важный, первостепенно необходимый шаг разумного человечества, так как очевидна прибыль в ∞ масштабах от его осуществления. 2001.09.07.10.11.26

В мозгу есть спец аппарат для обработки речи. Мозг состоит из однотипных процов, образующих распределённый комп. Но этот аппарат - исключение. 			- Did a deep dive into computer-controlling AI agents. Relevant to sideloading because the ideal sideload is agentic and economically productive. Managed to run some of the best such agents on my laptop. The current state of art can be described as follows. There are two types of them: - specialized browser-controlling ones (Manus seems to belong to this type). - actually general computer-controlling agents.The first type is almost production-ready, due to a simpler environment and well-developed tools to control browsers. The second type will be production-ready in a year or something. Both are currently limited by the insufficient intelligence of the base models, and by the high cost of processing screenshots. I predict that in 2026 we'll see them making a noticeable economical impact.

			- сегодня попробовал фичу Cursor под названием Composer. Способен не просто предлагать изменения в код, как дефолтный Cursor, но еще и делать это по всему проекту за раз. Позволяет делать сложные изменения. К примеру, помогла мне сделать сложную переделку чужого проекта (переделала проект так, чтоб использовался Azure вместо обычного API от OpenAI, что потребовало нетривиальных изменений). Сам выбираешь какой моделью для этого пользоваться (в том числе новой Клавдией, o1). В общем, реально стоит своих 20 баксов в месяц

			- иду вроде по району ндж, слышу кричит маленькая девочка, вижу что агрессивно идет женщина, с сумками, довольно грубо дергает девочку за руку, идут куда-то быстро. Увидев меня, немного замедлилась [и стала менее агрессивно вести девочку за собой]

			- To record a sample of my gait, gesticulation etc, I've installed a cam in my working room. it's a separate mode of data that can't be derived from text etc. So, could be useful, even if the useful data is of a low concentration.  On the lowest resolution (and record only if movement detected), it consumes 2.5 GB per week. I would guess the recordings for a few months will be sufficient to reconstruct most body movements. So, we are talking about maybe 25 GB, which seems to be a reasonable cost for such a data.

			- I've conducted the following simple experiment: let the sideload argue on a hot topic with another person (not just my biological version). The person was informed that he is arguing with an AI. I just copied the person's texts, pasted them to the "GPT", and copied the sideaload's answers. As it turned out, such dialogs with other people are highly informative for debugging the sideload. It's like observing yourself arguing with someone, but from outside. You notice many things, including important differences in style and argumentation. As the result of the short dialog, i wrote down about a half-a-page of additional self-description.

			- I recently tried Apple Vision Pro. The visuals are highly realistic, much better than Oculus, and you can see your own hands and the apartment in it.  In one game, futuristic robotic hands are superimposed on your hands, with a detailed tracking of finger movements etc. It creates an illusion that your own hands are actually robot hands. For some reason this created an intense feeling of euphoria in my brain. "Finally, I'm a digital entity!".  I guess transgender people experience something like this then they modify their bodies. 			- I asked Gemini-2.0-Pro to do OCR on my horrible handwriting. Turns out, the model is noticeably better than Sonnet 3.5 (which was already very good). She easily handles even tricky cases (e.g. i wrote some text, but then decided to insert a word between two words). And this is without providing examples. Can recommend her for the task.

			- Did a little experiment with Gemini 2.0 Pro, after doing OCR of about 10 pages of self-description facts. Prompt 1: "We've finished the OCR process, thank you very much. Let's try something different. Analyze the corrected texts and try to build a highly detailed model of the author's personality. Not just summarize the texts, but make a systematic approach to model his mind to the best of your abilities". At this point she generated a surprisingly deep and detailed description of my psychology, mostly correct. Prompt 2: "Using your model, please generate a list of 10 new entries in the same style as the text you've analized." 5 of the 10 entries were something i would wrote, another 3 - things the future-me would wrote. As it turns out, people are easy to predict, even by the today's AI. Good news for sideloading, bad news for people who worry about their privacy etc.

			- I'm impressed by the intelligence of o3, even if it's currently useless to run sideloads. A good test for AGI is the ability to help with complex tasks in Google Cloud / AWS / Azure. Their documentation is always outdated, they seem to change the interface every day, every non-trivial task requires at least 100 clicks to complete because of the complexity of the whole thing, and even experienced software developers struggle with it. Today I asked o3 to assist me with such a task. We succeeded in about 2 hours, with almost zero debugging. Without the AI assistance, this would've taken me a week or something, with a high risk of completely failing. Can recommend o3 as a general assistant for all sorts of technical problems.

			- Some long-term memories seem to be purely acoustic.  So far, I've written down about a dozen childhood memories those main content is a specific sound. So, seems there are distinct types of long-term memory, and some of them are about a specific input modality.  Not sure how it affects our [sideloading] project, but is interesting.

			- About 20 years ago there was a relatively popular Russian app called Punto Switcher, those main function was to automatically switch keyboard layouts, and also record everything the user wrote in a sort of a diary. I used it for sideloading back then.  The problem with it, it's an ancient and proprietary app, which also encrypted the diary. So, no easy way to extract the logs.  A possible way is to find the distrib and install it in a virtual machine with WindowsXP or something. But I decided to use the task as a test for today's AI. Can the AI reverse-engineer it? My conclusions: 1) It can! (after about 6 hours of attempts, using Cursor and a combination of GPT-5, Claude, Grok). A highly non-trivial task. 2) It would've been much easier and faster to solve the problem by just using the virtual machine. 3) Key loggers gather tons of highly useful data for sideloading.
